The Company posted quarterly revenue of $124.3 billion, up 4 percent year over year, and quarterly diluted earnings per share of $2.40, up 10 percent year over year.</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Helvetica',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%">&#8220;Today Apple is reporting our best quarter ever, with revenue of $124.3 billion, up 4 percent from a year ago,&#8221; said Tim Cook, Apple&#8217;s CEO. &#8220;We were thrilled to bring customers our best-ever lineup of products and services during the holiday season. Through the power of Apple silicon, we&#8217;re unlocking new possibilities for our users with Apple Intelligence, which makes apps and experiences even better and more personal. And we&#8217;re excited that Apple Intelligence will be available in even more languages this April.&#8221;</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Helvetica',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%">&#8220;Our record revenue and strong operating margins drove EPS to a new all-time record with double-digit growth and allowed us to return over $30 billion to shareholders,&#8221; said Kevan Parekh, Apple&#8217;s CFO. &#8220;We are also pleased that our installed base of active devices has reached a new all-time high across all products and geographic segments.&#8221;</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Helvetica',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%">Apple&#8217;s board of directors has declared a cash dividend of $0.25 per share of the Company&#8217;s common stock. The dividend is payable on February 13, 2025, to shareholders of record as of the close of business on February 10, 2025.</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Helvetica',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%">Apple will provide live streaming of its Q1 2025 financial results conference call beginning at 2&#58;00 p.m. PT on January 30, 2025 at apple.com&#47;investor&#47;earnings-call.
